{'id': 'GO:0000372', 'isObsolete': False, 'name': 'Group I intron splicing', 'definition': {'text': 'The splicing of Group I introns. This occurs by a ribozymic mechanism where the intron sequence forms a distinct 3D structure, characteristic of Group I introns and involved in determining the locations of the splice sites (there do not appear to be consensus splice site sequences) as well as having a role in catalyzing the splicing reactions, though protein factors are also required in vivo.
